 aaie jaane
 
 
 1
 agar aapke rishte main khatas aa jaae yaa wo tuutane kii kagaar par pahunch jaae to aapke liye yah jaananaa behad jaruri he ki aakhir aisa kyon ho rahaa hai

 2
 Do not get in touch with the person after the breakup

 aaie jaanate hai iske bare main
 
 
 The first line of wealth - the first line of the forehead which is very close to the eyebrows, the line of money is - the clearer and clearer this line is, the better the financial condition will be
 - is lakeer kaa tutaa hona yaa chota hona baar-baar aarthik sthiti main utaar chadhaav dikhaata he
 The second streak related to health - the second line after the line near the eyebrows, is the line of health - these lines become healthy by being thick and clean, thin and light and ill
 - is lakeer kaa tutaa hona yaa upar-neeche hona lambe samay tak chalane vaali beemaari kaa sanket detaa he

 Makes a person very fortunate
